#### `takeDamage` — `obj:takeDamage(amount, damage_type)`

Apply damage, factoring in resistance. Resistance is a multiplier (default 1.0).

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `amount` | `number` | The amount value. |
| `damage_type` | `string` | The damage type value. |

**Returns**: `number` — actual damage dealt

#### `newStatusEffect`

Object returned by the corresponding `newnewStatusEffect(...)` constructor, or constructed inline.

| Method | Signature | Description |
|--------|-----------|-------------|
| `getName` | `obj:getName()` | Returns the current Name value. |
| `getDuration` | `obj:getDuration()` | Returns the current Duration value. |
| `setDuration` | `obj:setDuration(v)` | Sets the Duration to the given value. |
| `getStacks` | `obj:getStacks()` | Returns the current Stacks value. |
| `setStacks` | `obj:setStacks(v)` | Sets the Stacks to the given value. |
| `tickTurn` | `obj:tickTurn()` | Tick one turn. |
| `isExpired` | `obj:isExpired()` | Is the effect expired?. |
| `getMeta` | `obj:getMeta(key)` | ── StatusEffect: metadata ops ──────────────────────────────────────── Get a metadata value from the status effect's data table. |

---

## `cardgame`

**Source**: `library/cardgame/init.lua`  
**Require**: `local cardgame = require("library.cardgame")`

Card game system: card types, cards, stacks (decks/hands/zones), slots, card pools, stack manager, deck builder, history, and card groups. Pure-Lua port of src/cardgame/.

### Module Functions

| Function | Signature | Description |
|----------|-----------|-------------|
| `defineCardType` | `cardgame.defineCardType(name, def)` | Register or overwrite a card type definition. |
| `getCardType` | `cardgame.getCardType(name)` | Look up a card type by name. |
| `getCardTypeNames` | `cardgame.getCardTypeNames()` | Get all registered type names. |
| `clearCardTypes` | `cardgame.clearCardTypes()` | Clear all card type definitions. |
| `newCardTypeDef` | `cardgame.newCardTypeDef(name)` | ── CardTypeDef ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a new card type definition (blueprint). |
| `newCard` | `cardgame.newCard(card_type)` | Create a new card instance. |
| `newStack` | `cardgame.newStack(name)` | Creates and returns a new Stack instance. |
| `newStackWithCapacity` | `cardgame.newStackWithCapacity(name, cap)` | Creates and returns a new Stack With Capacity instance. |
| `newSlot` | `cardgame.newSlot(name)` | Creates and returns a new Slot instance. |
| `newSlotWithCapacity` | `cardgame.newSlotWithCapacity(name, cap)` | Creates and returns a new Slot With Capacity instance. |
| `newCardPool` | `cardgame.newCardPool(name)` | Creates and returns a new Card Pool instance. |
| `newStackManager` | `cardgame.newStackManager()` | Creates and returns a new Stack Manager instance. |
| `newBuildEntry` | `cardgame.newBuildEntry(type_name, count)` | ── BuildEntry ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────. |
| `newDeckBuilder` | `cardgame.newDeckBuilder(name)` | Creates and returns a new Deck Builder instance. |
| `newStackHistory` | `cardgame.newStackHistory()` | Creates and returns a new Stack History instance. |
| `newStackHistoryWithMaxSize` | `cardgame.newStackHistoryWithMaxSize(max_size)` | Creates and returns a new Stack History With Max Size instance. |
| `newCardGroup` | `cardgame.newCardGroup(label, indices, score)` | Creates and returns a new Card Group instance. |
| `checkDeckLimit` | `cardgame.checkDeckLimit(cards)` | ── M. |
| `groupByCategory` | `cardgame.groupByCategory(items)` | ── Module-level analytics free functions ───────────────────────────── Group card-like items by category field. |
| `findAtLeastNOfStat` | `cardgame.findAtLeastNOfStat(items, stat, n)` | Return items where getStat(stat) >= n. |
| `findTagGroups` | `cardgame.findTagGroups(items)` | Return each unique tag that appears on more than one item, with the items list. |
| `sortedIndicesByStat` | `cardgame.sortedIndicesByStat(items, stat)` | Return 1-based indices sorted by a stat (ascending). |
| `sortedIndicesByCategory` | `cardgame.sortedIndicesByCategory(items)` | Return 1-based indices sorted by category (alphabetical). |

---

## `combat`

**Source**: `library/combat/init.lua`  
**Require**: `local combat = require("library.combat")`

Vehicle/turret/weapon combat system: collision groups, armor, chassis, turrets, weapons, projectiles, projectile pools, and the combat world. Pure-Lua port of src/combat/.

### Enums

| Name | Values | Description |
|------|--------|-------------|
| `M.ProjectileType` | `Ballistic`, `Homing`, `Ray`, `Area`, `Beam` | ── ProjectileType enum ─────────────────────────────────────────────────── |
| `M.ArmorZone` | `Front`, `Rear`, `Side` | ── ArmorZone enum ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── |

### Module Functions

| Function | Signature | Description |
|----------|-----------|-------------|
| `newCollisionGroupSet` | `combat.newCollisionGroupSet()` | Creates and returns a new Collision Group Set instance. |
| `newMountSlot` | `combat.newMountSlot(id, x, y, size_class)` | ── MountSlot ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────. |
| `newChassis` | `combat.newChassis(body_id, max_hp)` | Creates and returns a new Chassis instance. |
| `newTurret` | `combat.newTurret(body_id, joint_id)` | Creates and returns a new Turret instance. |
| `newWeapon` | `combat.newWeapon(name)` | Creates and returns a new Weapon instance. |
| `newProjectilePool` | `combat.newProjectilePool(pool_size, projectile_type)` | Creates and returns a new Projectile Pool instance. |
| `newCombatWorld` | `combat.newCombatWorld()` | Creates and returns a new Combat World instance. |

---

## `crafting`

**Source**: `library/crafting/init.lua`  
**Require**: `local crafting = require("library.crafting")`

Crafting system: recipes, ingredients, outputs, job queues, stations, craft skills, perk trees, upgrade trees, modifier pools, and recipe knowledge. Pure-Lua port of src/crafting/.

### Enums

| Name | Values | Description |
|------|--------|-------------|
| `M.Quality` | `Normal`, `Fine`, `Superior`, `Excellent`, `Masterwork`, `Legendary` | ── Quality enum ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── |

### Module Functions

| Function | Signature | Description |
|----------|-----------|-------------|
| `qualityFromStr` | `crafting.qualityFromStr(s)` | Convert string to Quality value. |
| `qualityToStr` | `crafting.qualityToStr(q)` | Quality to display string. |
| `newIngredient` | `crafting.newIngredient(item_type, quantity)` | Create ingredient by item type. |
| `newIngredientTag` | `crafting.newIngredientTag(tag, quantity)` | Create ingredient by tag. |
| `newRecipeOutput` | `crafting.newRecipeOutput(item_type, quantity)` | Creates and returns a new Recipe Output instance. |
| `newRecipeOutputWithChance` | `crafting.newRecipeOutputWithChance(item_type, quantity, chance)` | Creates and returns a new Recipe Output With Chance instance. |
| `newRecipe` | `crafting.newRecipe(id)` | Creates and returns a new Recipe instance. |
| `newRecipeRegistry` | `crafting.newRecipeRegistry()` | Creates and returns a new Recipe Registry instance. |
| `newCraftJob` | `crafting.newCraftJob(id, recipe_id, total_time, quantity)` | Creates and returns a new Craft Job instance. |
| `newCraftQueue` | `crafting.newCraftQueue(max_jobs)` | Creates and returns a new Craft Queue instance. |

| `canUse` | `obj:canUse(recipe)` | Return true if this skill satisfies a recipe's skill gate. |
| `recipeColor` | `obj:recipeColor(recipe)` | WoW-style difficulty colour for a recipe. |
| `skillUpChance` | `obj:skillUpChance(recipe)` | Probability (0-1) of a skill-up when crafting this recipe. |
| `addSpecialization` | `obj:addSpecialization(name)` | Register a specialization branch (no-op if already present). |
| `getSpecializations` | `obj:getSpecializations()` | Return the list of registered specialization branches. |
| `chooseSpecialization` | `obj:chooseSpecialization(name)` | Lock in a chosen specialization. |
| `getSpecialization` | `obj:getSpecialization()` | Return the current specialization (or nil if none). |
| `availablePerks` | `obj:availablePerks()` | Return perks available at the current skill level from the perk tree. |
| `getSpeedBonus` | `obj:getSpeedBonus()` | Computed speed bonus from unlocked perks. |
| `getQualityBonus` | `obj:getQualityBonus()` | Computed quality bonus from unlocked perks. |
| `getYieldBonus` | `obj:getYieldBonus()` | Computed yield bonus from unlocked perks. |

## `dialog`

**Source**: `library/dialog/init.lua`  
**Require**: `local dialog = require("library.dialog")`

Luna2D dialog sequencer — typewriter text, branching choices, events. A pure-Lua replacement for the former `luna.dialog` Rust binding. No engine dependencies; works in headless test VMs.

### Enums

| Name | Values | Description |
|------|--------|-------------|
| `M.NodeType` | `SAY`, `CHOICE`, `WAIT`, `EVENT`, `CALL`, `JUMP` | Dialog-graph node-type enum. |
| `M.SequencerState` | `IDLE`, `RUNNING`, `WAITING_CHOICE`, `DONE` | Sequencer runtime-state enum. |

### Module Functions

| Function | Signature | Description |
|----------|-----------|-------------|
| `newSequencer` | `dialog.newSequencer()` | Creates and returns a new Sequencer instance. |

#### `newSequencer` — `dialog.newSequencer()`

Creates and returns a new Sequencer instance. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `table` — Sequencer object.

### Types

#### `newSequencer`

Object returned by the corresponding `newnewSequencer(...)` constructor, or constructed inline.

| Method | Signature | Description |
|--------|-----------|-------------|
| `load` | `obj:load(nodes)` | ── public API ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Load a new script, replacing any existing one. |
| `start` | `obj:start()` | Begin playback from the first node. |
| `update` | `obj:update(dt)` | Advance per-frame. |
| `advance` | `obj:advance()` | Advance past the current line (when state == "waiting" or "typing"). |
| `skip` | `obj:skip()` | Skip the entire current line instantly (advances to "waiting"). |
| `choose` | `obj:choose(index)` | Select a choice option by 1-based index. |
| `setSpeed` | `obj:setSpeed(cps)` | Set the typewriter reveal speed. |
| `getSpeed` | `obj:getSpeed()` | Get the current reveal speed. |
| `getState` | `obj:getState()` | Get the current state string. |
| `isActive` | `obj:isActive()` | Returns true while the sequence is in progress (not idle or done). |
| `isWaitingForChoice` | `obj:isWaitingForChoice()` | Returns true when a choice is pending player input. |
| `currentSpeaker` | `obj:currentSpeaker()` | Returns the speaker name of the current "say" node. |
| `currentText` | `obj:currentText()` | Returns the full text of the current "say" node. |
| `revealedText` | `obj:revealedText()` | Returns only the revealed portion of the current text. |
| `getChoiceText` | `obj:getChoiceText()` | Returns the prompt text of the current "choice" node. |
| `getChoiceLabels` | `obj:getChoiceLabels()` | Returns an array of choice labels for the current "choice" node. |
| `on` | `obj:on(event, fn)` | Register a callback for a named event. |
| `off` | `obj:off(event)` | Unregister all callbacks for a named event. |

#### `load` — `obj:load(nodes)`

── public API ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Load a new script, replacing any existing one. Call start() afterwards to begin playback.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `nodes` | `table` | Array of node tables. |

#### `start` — `obj:start()`

Begin playback from the first node. Returns the result to the caller.

#### `update` — `obj:update(dt)`

Advance per-frame. Call every frame while isActive() is true.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `dt` | `number` | Delta time in seconds. |

#### `advance` — `obj:advance()`

Advance past the current line (when state == "waiting" or "typing"). If typing, skips to full reveal first. If waiting, moves to next node.

#### `skip` — `obj:skip()`

Skip the entire current line instantly (advances to "waiting"). Returns the result to the caller.

#### `choose` — `obj:choose(index)`

Select a choice option by 1-based index. Only valid when state == "choice".

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `index` | `number` | 1-based index into getChoiceLabels(). |

#### `setSpeed` — `obj:setSpeed(cps)`

Set the typewriter reveal speed. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `cps` | `number` | Characters per second (default: 20). |

#### `getSpeed` — `obj:getSpeed()`

Get the current reveal speed. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `number` — Characters per second.

#### `getState` — `obj:getState()`

Get the current state string. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `string` — One of: "idle", "typing", "waiting", "choice", "paused", "done".

#### `isActive` — `obj:isActive()`

Returns true while the sequence is in progress (not idle or done). Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `boolean`

#### `isWaitingForChoice` — `obj:isWaitingForChoice()`

Returns true when a choice is pending player input. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `boolean`

#### `currentSpeaker` — `obj:currentSpeaker()`

Returns the speaker name of the current "say" node. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `string`

#### `currentText` — `obj:currentText()`

Returns the full text of the current "say" node. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `string`

#### `revealedText` — `obj:revealedText()`

Returns only the revealed portion of the current text. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `string`

#### `getChoiceText` — `obj:getChoiceText()`

Returns the prompt text of the current "choice" node. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `string`

#### `getChoiceLabels` — `obj:getChoiceLabels()`

Returns an array of choice labels for the current "choice" node. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `table` — Array of strings.

#### `on` — `obj:on(event, fn)`

Register a callback for a named event. Events: "line" (speaker, text), "choice" (), "finished" ().

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `event` | `string` | Event name. |
| `fn` | `function` | Callback function. |

#### `off` — `obj:off(event)`

Unregister all callbacks for a named event. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `event` | `string` | Event name. |

#### `newManager`

Object returned by the corresponding `newnewManager(...)` constructor, or constructed inline.

| Method | Signature | Description |
|--------|-----------|-------------|
| `newResource` | `obj:newResource(name, capacity)` | Create (or return existing) resource. |
| `getResource` | `obj:getResource(name)` | Returns the current Resource value. |
| `hasResource` | `obj:hasResource(name)` | Returns true if the object has the specified Resource. |
| `getResourceNames` | `obj:getResourceNames()` | Returns the current Resource Names value. |
| `removeResource` | `obj:removeResource(name)` | Remove a resource by name. |
| `tick` | `obj:tick(dt)` | Tick all enabled resources and advance conversion rule cooldowns / modifiers. |
| `turn` | `obj:turn()` | Turn: equivalent to tick(1. |
| `addConversionRule` | `obj:addConversionRule(rule)` | Add a conversion rule. |
| `getConversionRules` | `obj:getConversionRules()` | Returns the current Conversion Rules value. |
| `convert` | `obj:convert(from, to, amount)` | Convert resources using the first matching rule. |
| `exchange` | `obj:exchange(other, give_name, give_amount, get_name, get_amount)` | Direct two-way exchange between two managers (atomic). |
| `totalByGroup` | `obj:totalByGroup(group)` | Sum of values for all resources in a group. |
| `getPercent` | `obj:getPercent(name)` | Percent full (0-100) for a resource, 0 if capacity <= 0. |
| `isFull` | `obj:isFull(name)` | Is the resource at capacity?. |
| `isEmpty` | `obj:isEmpty(name)` | Is the resource at minimum?. |
| `canAffordAll` | `obj:canAffordAll(needs)` | Check if all resources in the table can be afforded. |
| `spendAll` | `obj:spendAll(needs)` | Atomically spend all resources in the table. |
| `reset` | `obj:reset()` | Clear all resources and conversion rules. |
| `getValue` | `obj:getValue(name)` | Convenience accessors on manager (delegate to named resource). |
| `setValue` | `obj:setValue(name, v)` | Sets the Value to the given value. |
| `getCapacity` | `obj:getCapacity(name)` | Returns the current Capacity value. |
| `setCapacity` | `obj:setCapacity(name, c)` | Sets the Capacity to the given value. |
| `getMinimum` | `obj:getMinimum(name)` | Returns the current Minimum value. |
| `setMinimum` | `obj:setMinimum(name, m)` | Sets the Minimum to the given value. |
| `getFlowRate` | `obj:getFlowRate(name)` | Returns the current Flow Rate value. |
| `setFlowRate` | `obj:setFlowRate(name, rate)` | Sets the Flow Rate to the given value. |
| `getDecayRate` | `obj:getDecayRate(name)` | Returns the current Decay Rate value. |
| `setDecayRate` | `obj:setDecayRate(name, rate)` | Sets the Decay Rate to the given value. |
| `getDecayPercent` | `obj:getDecayPercent(name)` | Returns the current Decay Percent value. |
| `setDecayPercent` | `obj:setDecayPercent(name, pct)` | Sets the Decay Percent to the given value. |
| `getInterestRate` | `obj:getInterestRate(name)` | Returns the current Interest Rate value. |
| `setInterestRate` | `obj:setInterestRate(name, rate)` | Sets the Interest Rate to the given value. |
| `getUpkeep` | `obj:getUpkeep(name)` | Returns the current Upkeep value. |
| `setUpkeep` | `obj:setUpkeep(name, u)` | Sets the Upkeep to the given value. |
| `getNetRate` | `obj:getNetRate(name)` | Returns the current Net Rate value. |
| `getOverflow` | `obj:getOverflow(name)` | Returns the current Overflow value. |
| `setOverflow` | `obj:setOverflow(name, policy)` | Sets the Overflow to the given value. |
| `getGroup` | `obj:getGroup(name)` | Returns the current Group value. |
| `setGroup` | `obj:setGroup(name, g)` | Sets the Group to the given value. |
| `isEnabled` | `obj:isEnabled(name)` | Returns true if the object is currently enabled. |
| `setEnabled` | `obj:setEnabled(name, v)` | Sets the Enabled to the given value. |
| `isVisible` | `obj:isVisible(name)` | Returns true if the object is currently visible. |
| `setVisible` | `obj:setVisible(name, v)` | Sets the Visible to the given value. |
| `isLocked` | `obj:isLocked(name)` | Returns true if the object is currently locked. |
| `setLocked` | `obj:setLocked(name, v)` | Sets the Locked to the given value. |
| `add` | `obj:add(name, amount)` | Performs the add operation on the object. |
| `spend` | `obj:spend(name, amount)` | Performs the spend operation on the object. |
| `canAfford` | `obj:canAfford(name, amount)` | Performs the can afford operation on the object. |
| `getAvailable` | `obj:getAvailable(name)` | Returns the current Available value. |
| `reserveAmount` | `obj:reserveAmount(name, amount)` | Performs the reserve amount operation on the object. |
| `unreserveAmount` | `obj:unreserveAmount(name, amount)` | Performs the unreserve amount operation on the object. |
| `getReserved` | `obj:getReserved(name)` | Returns the current Reserved value. |

#### `newResource` — `obj:newResource(name, capacity)`

Create (or return existing) resource. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `name` | `string` | The name value. |
| `capacity` | `number` | The capacity value. |

**Returns**: `Resource`

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `name` | `string` | The name value. |

**Returns**: `Resource|nil`

| Parameter | Type | Description |

**Returns**: `boolean`

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `other` | `ResourceManager` | The other value. |
| `give_name` | `string` | Resource to give. |
| `give_amount` | `number` | The give amount value. |
| `get_name` | `string` | Resource to receive. |
| `get_amount` | `number` | The get amount value. |

**Returns**: `boolean`

#### `newModifier`

Object returned by the corresponding `newnewModifier(...)` constructor, or constructed inline.

| Method | Signature | Description |
|--------|-----------|-------------|
| `getType` | `obj:getType()` | Returns the current Type value. |
| `getValue` | `obj:getValue()` | Returns the current Value value. |
| `setValue` | `obj:setValue(v)` | Sets the Value to the given value. |
| `getDuration` | `obj:getDuration()` | Returns the current Duration value. |
| `getRemaining` | `obj:getRemaining()` | Returns the current Remaining value. |
| `getSource` | `obj:getSource()` | Returns the current Source value. |
| `getTarget` | `obj:getTarget()` | Returns the current Target value. |
| `setTarget` | `obj:setTarget(t)` | Sets the Target to the given value. |
| `isExpired` | `obj:isExpired()` | Returns true if the object is currently expired. |
| `isPermanent` | `obj:isPermanent()` | Returns true if the object is currently permanent. |
| `update` | `obj:update(dt)` | Updates the object state for the current frame or tick. |

#### `getType` — `obj:getType()`

Returns the current Type value. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `any`

#### `getValue` — `obj:getValue()`

Returns the current Value value. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `any`

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `v` | `any` | The v value. |

**Returns**: `any`

#### `getSource` — `obj:getSource()`

#### `newResource`

Object returned by the corresponding `newnewResource(...)` constructor, or constructed inline.

| Method | Signature | Description |
|--------|-----------|-------------|
| `_clamp` | `obj:_clamp(v)` | Clamp a value to [minimum, capacity]. |
| `getName` | `obj:getName()` | Returns the current Name value. |
| `getValue` | `obj:getValue()` | Returns the current Value value. |
| `setValue` | `obj:setValue(v)` | Set the resource value (clamped). |
| `getCapacity` | `obj:getCapacity()` | Returns the current Capacity value. |
| `setCapacity` | `obj:setCapacity(c)` | Set maximum capacity. |
| `getMinimum` | `obj:getMinimum()` | Returns the current Minimum value. |
| `setMinimum` | `obj:setMinimum(m)` | Set minimum value. |
| `getOverflow` | `obj:getOverflow()` | Returns the current Overflow value. |
| `setOverflow` | `obj:setOverflow(p)` | Set overflow policy. |
| `getFlowRate` | `obj:getFlowRate()` | Returns the current Flow Rate value. |
| `setFlowRate` | `obj:setFlowRate(r)` | Sets the Flow Rate to the given value. |
| `getDecayRate` | `obj:getDecayRate()` | Returns the current Decay Rate value. |
| `setDecayRate` | `obj:setDecayRate(r)` | Sets the Decay Rate to the given value. |
| `getDecayPercent` | `obj:getDecayPercent()` | Returns the current Decay Percent value. |
| `setDecayPercent` | `obj:setDecayPercent(p)` | Sets the Decay Percent to the given value. |
| `getInterestRate` | `obj:getInterestRate()` | Returns the current Interest Rate value. |
| `setInterestRate` | `obj:setInterestRate(r)` | Sets the Interest Rate to the given value. |
| `getUpkeep` | `obj:getUpkeep()` | Returns the current Upkeep value. |
| `setUpkeep` | `obj:setUpkeep(u)` | Sets the Upkeep to the given value. |
| `getGroup` | `obj:getGroup()` | Returns the current Group value. |
| `setGroup` | `obj:setGroup(g)` | Sets the Group to the given value. |
| `isEnabled` | `obj:isEnabled()` | Returns true if the object is currently enabled. |
| `setEnabled` | `obj:setEnabled(e)` | Sets the Enabled to the given value. |
| `isVisible` | `obj:isVisible()` | Returns true if the object is currently visible. |
| `setVisible` | `obj:setVisible(v)` | Sets the Visible to the given value. |
| `isLocked` | `obj:isLocked()` | Returns true if the object is currently locked. |
| `setLocked` | `obj:setLocked(l)` | Sets the Locked to the given value. |
| `getReserved` | `obj:getReserved()` | Returns the current Reserved value. |
| `getAvailable` | `obj:getAvailable()` | Returns the current Available value. |
| `getNetRate` | `obj:getNetRate()` | Net rate per tick (flow - decay - upkeep + interest - proportional_decay). |
| `add` | `obj:add(amount)` | Add amount to the resource. |
| `spend` | `obj:spend(amount)` | Spend an amount if available. |
| `canAfford` | `obj:canAfford(amount)` | Check if the resource can afford the amount. |
| `reserve` | `obj:reserve(amount)` | Reserve an amount (reduces available without changing value). |
| `unreserve` | `obj:unreserve(amount)` | Release a reservation. |
| `tick` | `obj:tick(dt)` | Advance the resource by dt seconds (flow, decay, interest, proportional decay). |

#### `_clamp` — `obj:_clamp(v)`

Clamp a value to [minimum, capacity]. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `v` | `any` | The v value. |

#### `getName` — `obj:getName()`

Returns the current Name value. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `string` — Resource name.

#### `getValue` — `obj:getValue()`

Returns the current Value value. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `number` — Current resource value.

#### `setValue` — `obj:setValue(v)`

Set the resource value (clamped). Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `v` | `number` | The v value. |

#### `getCapacity` — `obj:getCapacity()`

Returns the current Capacity value. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `number` — Capacity (-1 = unlimited).

#### `setCapacity` — `obj:setCapacity(c)`

Set maximum capacity. Re-clamps value.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `c` | `number` | The c value. |

#### `getMinimum` — `obj:getMinimum()`

Returns the current Minimum value. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `number` — Minimum value.

#### `setMinimum` — `obj:setMinimum(m)`

Set minimum value. Re-clamps value.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `m` | `number` | The m value. |

#### `getOverflow` — `obj:getOverflow()`

Returns the current Overflow value. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `string` — Overflow policy ("clamp", "lose", or "wrap").

#### `setOverflow` — `obj:setOverflow(p)`

Set overflow policy. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `p` | `string` | One of "clamp", "lose", "wrap". |

#### `getFlowRate` — `obj:getFlowRate()`

---

## `inventory`

**Source**: `library/inventory/init.lua`  
**Require**: `local inventory = require("library.inventory")`

### Enums

| Name | Values | Description |
|------|--------|-------------|
| `M.SlotState` | `Active`, `Passive`, `Idle` | ─── SlotState ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── |
| `M.ContainerMode` | `SLOTS`, `FIXED_GRID`, `FREE_GRID`, `BAG` | Container storage-mode enum. |

### Module Functions

| Function | Signature | Description |
|----------|-----------|-------------|
| `newItem` | `inventory.newItem(type_name)` | ─── InvItem ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a lightweight inventory item definition. |
| `newItemStack` | `inventory.newItemStack(inv_item, quantity, max_quantity)` | ─── ItemStack ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a counted stack of a single item type. |
| `newSlot` | `inventory.newSlot(slot_type, state)` | ─── Slot ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a single inventory slot (holds one ItemStack). |
| `newContainer` | `inventory.newContainer(name, mode, slot_count)` | ─── Container ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a named container managing a list of slots. |
| `newItemSet` | `inventory.newItemSet(name)` | ─── ItemSet ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a named item set (bonus condition). |
| `newInventory` | `inventory.newInventory()` | ─── Inventory ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a top-level inventory managing containers, equip slots, item sets, and subsystem flags. |

#### `newItem` — `inventory.newItem(type_name)`

─── InvItem ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a lightweight inventory item definition. Each item has a type, weight, size, stack limit, tag set, and a property map.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `type_name` | `string` | Item type identifier (e.g. "sword"). |

**Returns**: `table` — InvItem object.

#### `newItemStack` — `inventory.newItemStack(inv_item, quantity, max_quantity)`

─── ItemStack ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a counted stack of a single item type.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `inv_item` | `table` | InvItem definition. |
| `quantity` | `number` | Initial count. |
| `max_quantity` | `number` | Maximum stack size (clamped to >= 1). |

**Returns**: `table` — ItemStack object.

#### `newSlot` — `inventory.newSlot(slot_type, state)`

─── Slot ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a single inventory slot (holds one ItemStack).

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `slot_type` | `string` | Filter type ("any" = accept all). |
| `state` | `string` | SlotState value. |

**Returns**: `table` — Slot object.

#### `newContainer` — `inventory.newContainer(name, mode, slot_count)`

─── Container ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a named container managing a list of slots.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `name` | `string` | Container identifier. |
| `mode` | `string` | "fixed" | "unlimited" | "expandable" |
| `slot_count` | `number` | Initial number of slots (ignored for unlimited). |

**Returns**: `table` — Container object.

#### `newItemSet` — `inventory.newItemSet(name)`

─── ItemSet ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a named item set (bonus condition). All requirements must be satisfied simultaneously for the set to be active.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `name` | `string` | Display name. |

**Returns**: `table` — ItemSet object.

#### `newInventory` — `inventory.newInventory()`

─── Inventory ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a top-level inventory managing containers, equip slots, item sets, and subsystem flags.

**Returns**: `table` — Inventory object.

### Types

#### `newContainer`

Object returned by the corresponding `newnewContainer(...)` constructor, or constructed inline.

| Method | Signature | Description |
|--------|-----------|-------------|
| `getName` | `obj:getName()` | Return the container name. |
| `getMode` | `obj:getMode()` | Return the container mode string. |
| `slotCount` | `obj:slotCount()` | Return the number of slots. |
| `getCapacity` | `obj:getCapacity()` | Return max slot count. |
| `setWeightLimit` | `obj:setWeightLimit(w)` | Set weight limit. |
| `getWeightLimit` | `obj:getWeightLimit()` | Return weight limit. |
| `getCurrentWeight` | `obj:getCurrentWeight()` | Return current total weight. |
| `totalWeight` | `obj:totalWeight()` | Alias for getCurrentWeight. |
| `isFull` | `obj:isFull()` | Return true if all slots are occupied (fixed/expandable) or weight limit reached. |
| `getSlot` | `obj:getSlot(idx)` | Get a slot by 1-based index. |
| `getSlots` | `obj:getSlots()` | Return all slots array. |
| `addSlot` | `obj:addSlot(sl)` | Add slot (respects mode limits). |
| `expand` | `obj:expand(n)` | Expand by n new empty slots (expandable mode only). |
| `addItem` | `obj:addItem(inv_item, quantity)` | Auto-place item quantity. |
| `countItem` | `obj:countItem(type_name)` | Count all items of a given type across all slots. |
| `hasItem` | `obj:hasItem(type_name, qty)` | Return true if >= qty of type_name present. |
| `removeItem` | `obj:removeItem(type_name, qty)` | Remove up to qty items of type_name. |
| `findByTag` | `obj:findByTag(tag)` | Return all items with the given tag. |
| `toItemList` | `obj:toItemList()` | Return a summary list of {type_name, quantity} aggregated across slots. |
| `removeSlot` | `obj:removeSlot(idx)` | Remove the slot at a 1-based index. |

**Returns**: `number`

#### `transfer` — `obj:transfer(from_name, from_idx, to_name, to_idx)`

Transfer a stack from one container slot to another (1-based indices). Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `from_name` | `string` | Source container name. |
| `from_idx` | `number` | Source slot index (1-based). |
| `to_name` | `string` | Destination container name. |
| `to_idx` | `number` | Destination slot index (1-based). |

**Returns**: `boolean` — true on success

#### `splitStack` — `obj:splitStack(from_id, slot_idx, count, to_id)`

Split item count items out of container[from_container_id] at slot_idx into container[to_container_id]. Returns the overflow count (items that could not be moved).

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `from_id` | `string` | source container id |
| `slot_idx` | `number` | 1-based slot in source container |
| `count` | `number` | how many items to split |
| `to_id` | `string` | destination container id |

**Returns**: `number` — overflow count

#### `mergeStacks` — `obj:mergeStacks(container_id)`

Merge all stacks of the same item type in a container. Returns merge count.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `container_id` | `string` | The container id value. |

**Returns**: `number` — merges performed

#### `swap` — `obj:swap(container_a, slot_a, container_b, slot_b)`

Swap two slots (possibly across containers). Returns false if either slot is invalid.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `container_a` | `string` | The container a value. |
| `slot_a` | `number` | 1-based |
| `container_b` | `string` | The container b value. |
| `slot_b` | `number` | 1-based |

**Returns**: `boolean`

#### `newItem`

Object returned by the corresponding `newnewItem(...)` constructor, or constructed inline.

| Method | Signature | Description |
|--------|-----------|-------------|
| `getType` | `obj:getType()` | Return the type name. |
| `getWeight` | `obj:getWeight()` | Return item weight. |
| `setWeight` | `obj:setWeight(w)` | Set physical weight. |
| `getSizeW` | `obj:getSizeW()` | Return grid width. |
| `getSizeH` | `obj:getSizeH()` | Return grid height. |
| `setSize` | `obj:setSize(w, h)` | Set grid size. |
| `getStackLimit` | `obj:getStackLimit()` | Return maximum items per stack. |
| `setStackLimit` | `obj:setStackLimit(n)` | Set maximum stack size. |
| `hasTag` | `obj:hasTag(tag)` | Return true if the item has the given tag. |
| `addTag` | `obj:addTag(tag)` | Add a tag (no-op if already present). |
| `removeTag` | `obj:removeTag(tag)` | Remove a tag. |
| `getTags` | `obj:getTags()` | Return all tag names as an array. |

| `getProperty` | `obj:getProperty(key)` | Get a generic property. |
| `clone` | `obj:clone()` | Deep-copy this item definition. |

## `item`

**Source**: `library/item/init.lua`  
**Require**: `local item = require("library.item")`

| Name | Values | Description |

| `M.HistoryAction` | `Push`, `Pop`, `Clear`, `Custom` | ─── StackHistory ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── |

| `newItemPool` | `item.newItemPool()` | ─── Weighted item pool ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a weighted loot pool. |
| `newStackBuilder` | `item.newStackBuilder()` | ─── Stack builder ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a stack builder for constructing stacks from a recipe list. |
| `newStackHistory` | `item.newStackHistory(max_entries)` | Create a bounded event history for stack operations. |

#### `clearTypes` — `item.clearTypes()`

Clear all registered item types (useful between tests). Returns the result to the caller.

#### `defineType` — `item.defineType(name, def)`

Register a new item type definition. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `name` | `string` | Unique type name (e.g. "sword"). |
| `def` | `table` | { category="", base_stats={}, base_tags={} } |

#### `getType` — `item.getType(name)`

Retrieve a registered type definition, or nil. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `name` | `string` | The name value. |

**Returns**: `table|nil`

#### `getTypeNames` — `item.getTypeNames()`

Return a sorted list of all registered type names. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `table`

#### `newItem` — `item.newItem(type_name)`

─── Item object ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a new item instance. Stats and tags are copied from the type definition; modifications are per-instance.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `type_name` | `string` | Registered type name (or any string for ad-hoc items). |

**Returns**: `table` — Item object.

#### `newStack` — `item.newStack(name, capacity)`

─── Stack (LIFO with positional access) ───────────────────────────────────── Create a named stack with optional capacity limit. Acts as both a LIFO stack and a positional list.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `name` | `string` | Identifier for debugging. |
| `capacity` | `number` | Max item count. 0 = unlimited. |

**Returns**: `table` — Stack object.

#### `newItemPool` — `item.newItemPool()`

─── Weighted item pool ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a weighted loot pool. Supports weighted draw, bulk multi-draw, and unique-draw operations.

**Returns**: `table` — ItemPool object.

#### `newStackBuilder` — `item.newStackBuilder()`

─── Stack builder ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a stack builder for constructing stacks from a recipe list.

**Returns**: `table` — StackBuilder object.

#### `newStackHistory` — `item.newStackHistory(max_entries)`

Create a bounded event history for stack operations. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `max_entries` | `number` | Maximum entries to retain (default 50). |

**Returns**: `table` — StackHistory object.

#### `newStackManager` — `item.newStackManager()`

─── Stack manager ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a named-stack manager. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `table` — StackManager object.

#### `findNOfStat` — `item.findNOfStat(items, stat, n)`

─── Stat ranking ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Return 0-based indices of the top N items ranked by a stat (descending).

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `items` | `table` | Array of Item objects. |
| `stat` | `string` | Stat name. |
| `n` | `number` | How many to return. |

**Returns**: `table` — Array of 0-based integer indices.

#### `groupByStat` — `item.groupByStat(items, stat_key)`

─── Grouping helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Group items by a stat value. Returns map {value -> array of Items}. Items without the stat are grouped under the key false.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `items` | `table` | Array of Item objects. |
| `stat_key` | `string` | The stat key value. |

**Returns**: `table`

#### `groupByTagPrefix` — `item.groupByTagPrefix(items, prefix)`

Group items by tag prefix. Returns map {prefix_value -> array of Items}. A tag matches if it starts with `prefix` (e.g. prefix "tier:" matches "tier:1", "tier:2"). Items with no matching tag go under key "".

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `items` | `table` | Array of Item objects. |
| `prefix` | `string` | Tag prefix to filter on. |

**Returns**: `table`

#### `findSequences` — `item.findSequences(items, stat_key)`

Find runs (consecutive sequences) of items sharing the same stat value. Returns array of {value, start_idx, length} (1-based start_idx).

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `items` | `table` | Array of Item objects. |
| `stat_key` | `string` | The stat key value. |

**Returns**: `table`

#### `groupByCategory` — `item.groupByCategory(items)`

── Module-level free functions ──────────────────────────────────────── Group items by category. Returns table: category -> {Item, ...}.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `items` | `table` | list of Item objects |

**Returns**: `table`

#### `findAtLeastNOfStat` — `item.findAtLeastNOfStat(items, stat, n)`

Return items where getStat(stat) >= n. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `items` | `table` | The items value. |
| `stat` | `string` | The stat value. |
| `n` | `number` | The n value. |

**Returns**: `table`

#### `findTagGroups` — `item.findTagGroups(items)`

Group items by shared tag prefix. Returns table: prefix -> {Item, ...}. A "tag group" is a set of items that share at least one tag.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `items` | `table` | The items value. |

**Returns**: `table` — tag -> {Item, ...}

#### `sortedIndicesByStat` — `item.sortedIndicesByStat(items, stat)`

Return 1-based indices sorted by a stat (ascending). Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `items` | `table` | The items value. |
| `stat` | `string` | The stat value. |

**Returns**: `table` — indices

#### `sortedIndicesByCategory` — `item.sortedIndicesByCategory(items)`

Return 1-based indices sorted by category (alphabetical). Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `items` | `table` | The items value. |

**Returns**: `table` — indices

#### `newItemPool`

Object returned by the corresponding `newnewItemPool(...)` constructor, or constructed inline.

| Method | Signature | Description |
|--------|-----------|-------------|
| `size` | `obj:size()` | Return number of entries. |
| `getEntries` | `obj:getEntries()` | Return all entries as array of {type_name, weight}. |
| `addType` | `obj:addType(type_name, weight)` | Add a type with a given weight. |
| `setWeight` | `obj:setWeight(type_name, weight)` | Update the weight of the first matching entry. |
| `remove` | `obj:remove(type_name)` | Remove the first entry of type_name. |
| `draw` | `obj:draw()` | Draw one random item (weighted). |
| `drawTypes` | `obj:drawTypes(n)` | Draw n items (with replacement). |
| `drawUniqueTypes` | `obj:drawUniqueTypes(n)` | Draw up to n unique type names (no type drawn twice), returns array of Items. |

#### `size` — `obj:size()`

Return number of entries. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `number`

#### `getEntries` — `obj:getEntries()`

Return all entries as array of {type_name, weight}. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `table`

#### `addType` — `obj:addType(type_name, weight)`

Add a type with a given weight. If type already present, adds another entry.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `type_name` | `string` | The type name value. |
| `weight` | `number` | The weight value. |

#### `setWeight` — `obj:setWeight(type_name, weight)`

Update the weight of the first matching entry. Returns false if not found.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `type_name` | `string` | The type name value. |
| `weight` | `number` | The weight value. |

**Returns**: `boolean`

#### `remove` — `obj:remove(type_name)`

Remove the first entry of type_name. Returns false if not found.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `type_name` | `string` | The type name value. |

**Returns**: `boolean`

#### `draw` — `obj:draw()`

Draw one random item (weighted). Returns "unknown" item if pool empty.

**Returns**: `table` — Item object

#### `drawTypes` — `obj:drawTypes(n)`

Draw n items (with replacement). Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `n` | `number` | The n value. |

**Returns**: `table` — Array of Item objects

#### `drawUniqueTypes` — `obj:drawUniqueTypes(n)`

Draw up to n unique type names (no type drawn twice), returns array of Items. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `n` | `number` | The n value. |

**Returns**: `table`

#### `newStack`

| `setCapacity` | `obj:setCapacity(n)` | Set or update capacity (0 = unlimited). |
| `isFull` | `obj:isFull()` | Return true if at capacity. |
| `clear` | `obj:clear()` | Remove all items. |
| `push` | `obj:push(it)` | ── Push / Pop (LIFO top) ────────────────────────────────────────────── Push item onto top (nil if capacity full, returns item if failed). |

| `pop` | `obj:pop()` | Pop and return top item, or nil if empty. |

| `popBottom` | `obj:popBottom()` | Remove and return bottom item, or nil if empty. |
| `peek` | `obj:peek()` | Peek at top item without removing it. |
| `getItem` | `obj:getItem()` | Alias for peek (slot compat). |

| `removeAt` | `obj:removeAt(idx)` | Remove and return item at 1-based index. |

| `findFirst` | `obj:findFirst(pred)` | Return the first item for which predicate(item) is true. |
| `getItems` | `obj:getItems()` | Return a shallow copy of all items (bottom to top). |
| `isEmpty` | `obj:isEmpty()` | Return true if the stack has no items. |
| `popMany` | `obj:popMany(n)` | Pop n items from the top. |
| `moveWithin` | `obj:moveWithin(from, to)` | Move item at index `from` to index `to` (both 1-based). |
| `searchByType` | `obj:searchByType(type_name)` | Return all items whose type matches. |
| `searchByTag` | `obj:searchByTag(tag)` | Return all items that have the given tag. |
| `searchByCategory` | `obj:searchByCategory(cat)` | Return all items in the given category. |

| `sortByStatDesc` | `obj:sortByStatDesc(stat)` | Sort items descending by a numeric stat. |

| `sortByName` | `obj:sortByName()` | Sort items by type name (alphabetical). |

| `peekTopNTypes` | `obj:peekTopNTypes(n)` | Return the type names of the top n items (without removing). |

| `extractAllBorders` | `province_map.extractAllBorders(map)` | Extract border segments for all adjacency edges. |
| `extractBordersWithTag` | `province_map.extractBordersWithTag(map, tag)` | Extract border segments for edges that have a specific tag. |
| `calculateCapital` | `province_map.calculateCapital(map, id)` | Get the centroid position of the province as the capital point. |
| `calculateAllPositions` | `province_map.calculateAllPositions(map)` | Set all province center positions to their centroid. |
| `totalEdgeCount` | `province_map.totalEdgeCount(map)` | Count total adjacency edges across all provinces in the map. |
| `allFactions` | `province_map.allFactions(map)` | Get all unique faction names present in the map. |
| `extractBordersByProperty` | `province_map.extractBordersByProperty(map, prop_fn)` | Return all adjacency pairs where prop_fn(provinceA) ~= prop_fn(provinceB). |
| `detectAdjacencyWithTags` | `province_map.detectAdjacencyWithTags(map, tags)` | Return adjacency pairs where BOTH provinces share ALL tags in the given tags list. |
| `adjacencyToGraph` | `province_map.adjacencyToGraph(map)` | Convert a province map's adjacency structure to a generic graph representation. |

#### `newFixedColorFn` — `province_map.newFixedColorFn(province_colors)`

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `province_colors` | `table` | {[id] = {r, g, b}} |

**Returns**: `table`

| `values` | `table` | {[id] = number} |

| `max_val` | `number` | The max val value. |

**Returns**: `table`

#### `findRoute` — `obj:findRoute(from_id, to_id, passable_fn)`

BFS route from province `from_id` to `to_id`. Returns an ordered list of province IDs forming the path, or nil if unreachable. Passable edges (passable == true) and optional cost filter are respected.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `from_id` | `number` | The from id value. |
| `to_id` | `number` | The to id value. |
| `passable_fn` | `function|nil` | passable_fn(edge) → boolean (nil = all passable) |

**Returns**: `table|nil` — ordered province ID list including from_id and to_id

## `quest`

**Source**: `library/quest/init.lua`  
**Require**: `local quest = require("library.quest")`

### Enums

| Name | Values | Description |
|------|--------|-------------|
| `M.QuestStatus` | `LOCKED`, `ACTIVE`, `COMPLETED`, `FAILED` | Quest lifecycle status enum. |
| `M.ObjectiveStatus` | `LOCKED`, `ACTIVE`, `COMPLETED`, `FAILED` | Objective completion-state enum. |

### Module Functions

| Function | Signature | Description |
|----------|-----------|-------------|
| `newObjective` | `quest.newObjective(id, description, required)` | Create a new objective with 0/required progress. |
| `newQuestStage` | `quest.newQuestStage(id, name)` | Create a new empty quest stage. |
| `newQuest` | `quest.newQuest(id, title)` | Create a new quest in the "available" state. |
| `newQuestLog` | `quest.newQuestLog()` | Create an empty quest log. |

#### `newObjective` — `quest.newObjective(id, description, required)`

Create a new objective with 0/required progress. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `id` | `string` | Unique identifier within the parent quest. |
| `description` | `string` | Human-readable display text. |
| `required` | `number` | Required count to mark as done. |

**Returns**: `Objective`

#### `newQuestStage` — `quest.newQuestStage(id, name)`

Create a new empty quest stage. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `id` | `string` | Unique stage identifier. |
| `name` | `string` | Display name for this stage. |

**Returns**: `QuestStage`

#### `newQuest` — `quest.newQuest(id, title)`

Create a new quest in the "available" state. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `id` | `string` | Unique identifier. |
| `title` | `string` | Display title. |

**Returns**: `Quest`

#### `newQuestLog` — `quest.newQuestLog()`

Create an empty quest log. Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `QuestLog`

### Types

#### `newObjective`

Object returned by the corresponding `newnewObjective(...)` constructor, or constructed inline.

| Method | Signature | Description |
|--------|-----------|-------------|
| `advance` | `obj:advance(amount)` | Advance progress by amount. |
| `setProgress` | `obj:setProgress(value)` | Set progress directly. |
| `isComplete` | `obj:isComplete()` | Returns true if this objective is considered complete (done or skipped). |
| `addTag` | `obj:addTag(tag)` | Add a tag. |
| `hasTag` | `obj:hasTag(tag)` | Returns true if the given tag is present. |
| `removeTag` | `obj:removeTag(tag)` | Remove a tag from this objective. |

#### `advance` — `obj:advance(amount)`

Advance progress by amount. Automatically marks the objective as "done" when current >= required. Does nothing if already done or failed.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `amount` | `number` | Amount to advance (default 1). |

**Returns**: `number` — New progress value.

#### `setProgress` — `obj:setProgress(value)`

Set progress directly. Clamps to [0, required].

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `value` | `number` | New progress value. |

#### `isComplete` — `obj:isComplete()`

Returns true if this objective is considered complete (done or skipped). Returns the result to the caller.

**Returns**: `boolean`

#### `addTag` — `obj:addTag(tag)`

Add a tag. Has no effect if already present.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `tag` | `string` | Tag to add. |

#### `hasTag` — `obj:hasTag(tag)`

Returns true if the given tag is present. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `tag` | `string` | Tag to check. |

**Returns**: `boolean`

#### `removeTag` — `obj:removeTag(tag)`

Remove a tag from this objective. Returns true if the tag was present.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `tag` | `string` | The tag value. |

**Returns**: `boolean`

| `start` | `obj:start()` | Start the quest (transition from "available" to "active"). |

| `activeObjectiveIds` | `obj:activeObjectiveIds()` | Returns the IDs of all objectives currently "active" across all stages. |
| `resetObjective` | `obj:resetObjective(id)` | Reset an objective back to "active" (in progress). |
| `allObjectivesComplete` | `obj:allObjectivesComplete()` | Return true if every mandatory objective in the quest is complete. |

---

## `stats`

**Source**: `library/stats/init.lua`  
**Require**: `local stats = require("library.stats")`

RPG character stat sheets with attributes, buffs, skills, perks, traits, XP/levelling, action points, morale, resistances, encumbrance and initiative. Pure-Lua port of src/stats/.

### Enums

| Name | Values | Description |
|------|--------|-------------|
| `M.StackMode` | `None`, `Duration`, `Intensity` | ── Enums ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── |

### Module Functions

| Function | Signature | Description |
|----------|-----------|-------------|
| `newAttribute` | `stats.newAttribute(base)` | Create a new attribute. |
| `newBuff` | `stats.newBuff(stat, add, mul, duration, source)` | Create a new buff. |
| `newSkill` | `stats.newSkill(opts)` | Create a new skill. |
| `newPerk` | `stats.newPerk(opts)` | Create a new perk. |
| `newActionPoints` | `stats.newActionPoints(max_val)` | Creates and returns a new Action Points instance. |
| `newMorale` | `stats.newMorale(max_val)` | Creates and returns a new Morale instance. |
| `newTableThresholds` | `stats.newTableThresholds(values)` | Create table-based thresholds. |
| `newLinearThresholds` | `stats.newLinearThresholds(base, increment)` | Create linear thresholds (base + (level-1)*increment). |
| `newTraitDef` | `stats.newTraitDef(buffs)` | ── TraitDef ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Create a trait definition. |
| `defineTrait` | `stats.defineTrait(name, def)` | Register a trait definition. |
| `defineRace` | `stats.defineRace(name, def)` | Register a race archetype. |
| `defineClass` | `stats.defineClass(name, def)` | Register a class archetype. |
| `getTraitNames` | `stats.getTraitNames()` | Get registered trait names. |
| `getRaceNames` | `stats.getRaceNames()` | Get registered race names. |
| `getClassNames` | `stats.getClassNames()` | Get registered class names. |
| `applyArchetypes` | `stats.applyArchetypes(sheet, race_name, class_name)` | Apply race and/or class archetypes to a sheet. |
| `newSheet` | `stats.newSheet()` | Create a new character sheet. |

| `addBuff` | `obj:addBuff(stat, add, mul, duration, source)` | ── Buffs ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Add a buff, returns handle. |
| `removeBuff` | `obj:removeBuff(handle)` | Remove a buff by handle. |
| `clearBuffs` | `obj:clearBuffs(stat)` | Clear all buffs or only those matching stat. |
| `getBuffs` | `obj:getBuffs(stat)` | Get active buffs as an array of info tables. |
| `getBuffCount` | `obj:getBuffCount(stat)` | Count active buffs (optionally filtered by stat). |
| `applyTraitBuffs` | `obj:applyTraitBuffs(trait_name)` | ── Traits ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Apply trait buffs (permanent) from the registry. |
| `removeTraitBuffs` | `obj:removeTraitBuffs(trait_name)` | Remove trait buffs. |
| `hasTrait` | `obj:hasTrait(name)` | Returns true if the object has the specified Trait. |
| `getActiveTraits` | `obj:getActiveTraits()` | Returns the current Active Traits value. |
| `defineSkill` | `obj:defineSkill(name, opts)` | ── Skills ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────. |
| `learnSkill` | `obj:learnSkill(name)` | Performs the learn skill operation on the object. |
| `useSkill` | `obj:useSkill(name)` | Performs the use skill operation on the object. |
| `getSkillLevel` | `obj:getSkillLevel(name)` | Returns the current Skill Level value. |
| `getCooldownRemaining` | `obj:getCooldownRemaining(name)` | Returns the current Cooldown Remaining value. |
| `definePerk` | `obj:definePerk(name, opts)` | ── Perks ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────. |
| `acquirePerk` | `obj:acquirePerk(name)` | Performs the acquire perk operation on the object. |
| `hasPerk` | `obj:hasPerk(name)` | Returns true if the object has the specified Perk. |
| `setFlag` | `obj:setFlag(name)` | ── Flags ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────. |
| `clearFlag` | `obj:clearFlag(name)` | Clears all flag entries. |
| `hasFlag` | `obj:hasFlag(name)` | Returns true if the object has the specified Flag. |
| `getFlags` | `obj:getFlags()` | Returns the current Flags value. |
| `addXP` | `obj:addXP(amount)` | ── XP / Level ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────. |
| `getXP` | `obj:getXP()` | Returns the current X P value. |
| `setXP` | `obj:setXP(v)` | Sets the X P to the given value. |
| `getLevel` | `obj:getLevel()` | Returns the current Level value. |
| `setLevel` | `obj:setLevel(v)` | Sets the Level to the given value. |
| `setLevelThresholds` | `obj:setLevelThresholds(t)` | Sets the Level Thresholds to the given value. |
| `recordUse` | `obj:recordUse(name)` | ── Use tracking ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────. |
| `getUseCount` | `obj:getUseCount(name)` | Returns the current Use Count value. |
| `setActionPoints` | `obj:setActionPoints(max_val)` | ── Action Points ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────. |

#### `define` — `obj:define(name, base, opts)`

── Attributes ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── Define a named attribute. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `name` | `string` | Attribute name. |
| `base` | `number` | Base value. |
| `opts` | `table|nil` | Optional: min, max, regen, growth. |

#### `get` — `obj:get(name)`

Get effective value (base + buffs, clamped). Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `name` | `string` | The name value. |

**Returns**: `number|nil`

#### `getBase` — `obj:getBase(name)`

Get raw base value. Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `name` | `string` | The name value. |

**Returns**: `any`

#### `setBase` — `obj:setBase(name, value)`

Set base value (clamped to min/max). Returns the result to the caller.

**Parameters**

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `name` | `string` | The name value. |
| `value` | `number` | The value value. |

| Parameter | Type | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| `name` | `string` | The name value. |
| `val` | `any` | The val value. |
